data-reactid="1327"><div data-reactid="1328"><!-- react-text: 1329 --><!-- /react-text --><div data-reactid="1330">Welcome…

We have a lovely brick home centrally located in the chic, hip and trendy Royal Oak | Berkley, with convenient access to I-696, I-75, Southfield, Lodge and all expressways, you can easily get to Detroit and surrounding areas.  We try our best to make our home a comfortable, convenient and safe place for you to stay and we're proud at our 200+ guests and their positive reviews.  We welcome you to stay.

Our home is pet-free and smoke-free.

The Neighborhood…

Royal Oak | Berkley is an up-scale suburb outside of Detroit.  It is extremely safe and in fact one of the safest neighborhoods you can find.  Neighbors are typically professionals and starting families.  Within a mile is Woodward Avenue, famous for the Woodward Dream Cruise, which boasts a variety of restaurants, bars, grocery stores and everything you could imagine.

Detroit Airport
…is about 45-90 minutes away depending upon traffic, as the Airport is located in the middle of nowhere.

Downtown Detroit, Windsor|Ontario Canada and the Detroit Casinos
…are a quick 15-20 minutes down highway I-75.

Beaumont Hospital
…is 5-10 minutes away, and even some neighbors walk to work there.

Other Hospitals | Rochester | Pontiac | Auburn Hills
…are 30-40 minutes away, if that's too long, consider our other listing “LakeHouse" which is closer to these

The Room…

One Double Size bed, located on the main level.

Access…

Electronic access, come and go as you please.

The Home…

Fully stocked Living Room and Kitchen with TV, WiFi internet, dishes, pots, pans and more.  Towels, washer, dryer and even the laundry soap provided!

Parking…

One parking space is included.

Getting around…

Cars are very convenient.  Taxis and buses are not as convenient but we do have them.  Download the Smart Bus schedule and maps if you plan to use public transportation.

Book early to avoid disappointment.  Our rooms always fill up!

We look forward to hosting you and welcome to Michigan!</div><!-- react-text: 1331 --><!-- /react-text --><div data-reactid="1332"><li data-reactid="1333"><p data-reactid="1334">Nice house et nice roommates !
